<script type="text/javascript">
    
      function addToCart(addUrl){
    $.ajax({
      url: "https://www.fantasygrounds.com/store/addtocartmenuAB.php" + addUrl,
      type: 'GET',

     })
     .done(function(response ) {
         //response - this is the response from the server
        // Refresh Cart indicator here 
        //location.reload();       
        $('#ShoppingCartMenu').html(response);
        alert("Shopping Cart Updated");
        
     });
 }

</script>

<script>
// Data passed from PHP
var saleStartDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleEndDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleDiscount = ;
var majorSale = ;
var originalPrice = ;
var newPrice = originalPrice * (1 - saleDiscount); 
var now = new Date().getTime();

// Add the sale indicator for licenses
var discountDiv = document.getElementById("license-sale-callout");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (discountDiv) {
		var percentOff  = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
		
		discountDiv.innerHTML = percentOff  + "% OFF";
		discountDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
	}
} else {
	discountDiv.classList.add("hidden");
}

// Add the correct price
var licensePrice = document.getElementById("licensePrice");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (licensePrice) {
		licensePrice.innerText = newPrice.toFixed(2);
	}
}

// Add the timer that tells when the sale ends
var x = setInterval(function() {
  var now = new Date().getTime();
  var targetDiv = document.getElementById("sale-timer-countdown");

  if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	targetDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
    var distance = saleEndDate - now;
    
    var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);

    var percent = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
    
    var existingBanner = document.getElementById("sale-message");

    if (!existingBanner && targetDiv) {
      var salePara = document.createElement("p");
      salePara.id = "sale-message";
	  salePara.innerHTML = "ENDS in <span id='sale-countdown'></span>";
	  targetDiv.insertBefore(salePara, targetDiv.firstChild);
    }

    var countdownSpan = document.getElementById("sale-countdown");
    if (countdownSpan) {
      countdownSpan.innerText = days + "d " + hours + "h " + minutes + "m " + seconds + "s";
    }

  } else {
	targetDiv.classList.add("hidden");
    clearInterval(x);
    var banner = document.getElementById("sale-message");
    if (banner) {
      banner.remove();
    }
  }
}, 1000);
</script>

  <section class="hero-section">
    <div data-delay="8000" data-animation="slide" class="slider w-slider" data-autoplay="true" data-easing="ease" data-hide-arrows="false" data-disable-swipe="false" data-autoplay-limit="0" data-nav-spacing="8" data-duration="500" data-infinite="true">
      <div class="w-slider-mask">
        <div class="slide w-slide">
          <div class="slide-container">
            <div class="slide-text-block">

<script>
// Data passed from PHP
var saleStartDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleEndDate = new Date("").getTime();
var saleDiscount = ;
var majorSale = ;
var originalPrice = ;
var newPrice = originalPrice * (1 - saleDiscount); 
var now = new Date().getTime();

// Add the sale indicator for licenses
var discountDiv = document.getElementById("license-sale-callout");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (discountDiv) {
		var percentOff  = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
		
		discountDiv.innerHTML = percentOff  + "% OFF";
		discountDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
	}
} else {
	discountDiv.classList.add("hidden");
}

// Add the correct price
var licensePrice = document.getElementById("licensePrice");
if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	if (licensePrice) {
		licensePrice.innerText = newPrice.toFixed(2);
	}
}

// Add the timer that tells when the sale ends
var x = setInterval(function() {
  var now = new Date().getTime();
  var targetDiv = document.getElementById("sale-timer-countdown");

  if (now >= saleStartDate && now <= saleEndDate) {
	targetDiv.classList.remove("hidden");
    var distance = saleEndDate - now;
    
    var days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    var hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
    var minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
    var seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);

    var percent = Math.round(saleDiscount * 100);
    
    var existingBanner = document.getElementById("sale-message");

    if (!existingBanner && targetDiv) {
      var salePara = document.createElement("p");
      salePara.id = "sale-message";
	  salePara.innerHTML = "ENDS in <span id='sale-countdown'></span>";
	  targetDiv.insertBefore(salePara, targetDiv.firstChild);
    }

    var countdownSpan = document.getElementById("sale-countdown");
    if (countdownSpan) {
      countdownSpan.innerText = days + "d " + hours + "h " + minutes + "m " + seconds + "s";
    }

  } else {
	targetDiv.classList.add("hidden");
    clearInterval(x);
    var banner = document.getElementById("sale-message");
    if (banner) {
      banner.remove();
    }
  }
}, 1000);
</script>

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=4920',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("Now Drafting").show();
	  else
	  // if > 85% go red
	  // if > 66% go yellow
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
	  //$(".GaugeMeter").gaugeMeter({ text: json['entries'] + ' / ' + json['max_entries'] });
   });
});

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=924',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['no_meter']) return;
	  if ('true' != json['open']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Starts " + json['open']).addClass('comingsoon').show();
	  else if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Playoff Drafts").show();
	  else
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
   });
   requestAnimationFrame(animate);
});

    const rotatingDiv = document.getElementById("rotatingDiv");

    let startTime = null;
    const amplitude = 3; // Maximum rotation angle in degrees
    const frequency = 1; // Oscillations per second

    // Animation function
    function animate(timestamp) {
      if (!startTime) startTime = timestamp;
      const elapsedTime = (timestamp - startTime) / 1000; // Convert to seconds

      // Calculate the rotation angle using a sine wave
      const angle = -45 + amplitude * Math.sin(2 * Math.PI * frequency * elapsedTime);

      // Apply the rotation angle to the div using CSS transform
      $('div[game=924] .sellout').css('transform','rotate(' + angle + 'deg)');

      // Continue the animation
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
	}

</script></div><div class="game-card col-xxl-3 col-xl-4 col-md-6 col-12 mx-auto"><div class="card mx-auto">

<script>
	
$(document).ready(function(){
   const $cols = $('.games-row .game-card');
   let groupSize = 1;
   let index = 0;
   function ShowGroup(start) {
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;
         
      $cols.hide();
      //if (start + groupSize >= $cols.length) index = 0;
      
//$('#theindex').html(index + '/' + $cols.length);

      for (let i = 0; i < groupSize; i++) {
         const current = (start + i) % $cols.length;
         $cols.eq(current).fadeIn(500);
      }
   }
   
   ShowGroup(index);
   
   var rotater = setInterval(() => {
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
     ShowGroup(index);
   }, 5000);
   
   $(window).on( "resize", function() { 
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;   
      ShowGroup(index); 
   });   

   $('.btn-left').click(function(){
 	   clearInterval(rotater);
      index = (index - groupSize) % $cols.length;
      if (index < 0) index = ($cols.length - index) % $cols.length;
	   ShowGroup(index);
   });

   $('.btn-right').click(function(){
	  clearInterval(rotater);
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
	  ShowGroup(index);
   });
   
   $('.ribbon h4').click(function(){
 	  window.location = '/tfc';
   });

});
</script>

$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=4920',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("Now Drafting").show();
	  else
	  // if > 85% go red
	  // if > 66% go yellow
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
	  //$(".GaugeMeter").gaugeMeter({ text: json['entries'] + ' / ' + json['max_entries'] });
   });
});

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=924',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['no_meter']) return;
	  if ('true' != json['open']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Starts " + json['open']).addClass('comingsoon').show();
	  else if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Playoff Drafts").show();
	  else
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
   });
   requestAnimationFrame(animate);
});

    const rotatingDiv = document.getElementById("rotatingDiv");

    let startTime = null;
    const amplitude = 3; // Maximum rotation angle in degrees
    const frequency = 1; // Oscillations per second

    // Animation function
    function animate(timestamp) {
      if (!startTime) startTime = timestamp;
      const elapsedTime = (timestamp - startTime) / 1000; // Convert to seconds

      // Calculate the rotation angle using a sine wave
      const angle = -45 + amplitude * Math.sin(2 * Math.PI * frequency * elapsedTime);

      // Apply the rotation angle to the div using CSS transform
      $('div[game=924] .sellout').css('transform','rotate(' + angle + 'deg)');

      // Continue the animation
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
	}

</script></div><div class="game-card col-xxl-3 col-xl-4 col-md-6 col-12 mx-auto"><div class="card mx-auto">

<script>
	
$(document).ready(function(){
   const $cols = $('.games-row .game-card');
   let groupSize = 1;
   let index = 0;
   function ShowGroup(start) {
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;
         
      $cols.hide();
      //if (start + groupSize >= $cols.length) index = 0;
      
//$('#theindex').html(index + '/' + $cols.length);

      for (let i = 0; i < groupSize; i++) {
         const current = (start + i) % $cols.length;
         $cols.eq(current).fadeIn(500);
      }
   }
   
   ShowGroup(index);
   
   var rotater = setInterval(() => {
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
     ShowGroup(index);
   }, 5000);
   
   $(window).on( "resize", function() { 
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;   
      ShowGroup(index); 
   });   

   $('.btn-left').click(function(){
 	   clearInterval(rotater);
      index = (index - groupSize) % $cols.length;
      if (index < 0) index = ($cols.length - index) % $cols.length;
	   ShowGroup(index);
   });

   $('.btn-right').click(function(){
	  clearInterval(rotater);
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
	  ShowGroup(index);
   });
   
   $('.ribbon h4').click(function(){
 	  window.location = '/tfc';
   });

});
</script>

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=4920',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("Now Drafting").show();
	  else
	  // if > 85% go red
	  // if > 66% go yellow
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
	  //$(".GaugeMeter").gaugeMeter({ text: json['entries'] + ' / ' + json['max_entries'] });
   });
});

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=924',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['no_meter']) return;
	  if ('true' != json['open']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Starts " + json['open']).addClass('comingsoon').show();
	  else if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Playoff Drafts").show();
	  else
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
   });
   requestAnimationFrame(animate);
});

    const rotatingDiv = document.getElementById("rotatingDiv");

    let startTime = null;
    const amplitude = 3; // Maximum rotation angle in degrees
    const frequency = 1; // Oscillations per second

    // Animation function
    function animate(timestamp) {
      if (!startTime) startTime = timestamp;
      const elapsedTime = (timestamp - startTime) / 1000; // Convert to seconds

      // Calculate the rotation angle using a sine wave
      const angle = -45 + amplitude * Math.sin(2 * Math.PI * frequency * elapsedTime);

      // Apply the rotation angle to the div using CSS transform
      $('div[game=924] .sellout').css('transform','rotate(' + angle + 'deg)');

      // Continue the animation
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
	}

</script></div><div class="game-card col-xxl-3 col-xl-4 col-md-6 col-12 mx-auto"><div class="card mx-auto">

<script>
	
$(document).ready(function(){
   const $cols = $('.games-row .game-card');
   let groupSize = 1;
   let index = 0;
   function ShowGroup(start) {
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;
         
      $cols.hide();
      //if (start + groupSize >= $cols.length) index = 0;
      
//$('#theindex').html(index + '/' + $cols.length);

      for (let i = 0; i < groupSize; i++) {
         const current = (start + i) % $cols.length;
         $cols.eq(current).fadeIn(500);
      }
   }
   
   ShowGroup(index);
   
   var rotater = setInterval(() => {
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
     ShowGroup(index);
   }, 5000);
   
   $(window).on( "resize", function() { 
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;   
      ShowGroup(index); 
   });   

   $('.btn-left').click(function(){
 	   clearInterval(rotater);
      index = (index - groupSize) % $cols.length;
      if (index < 0) index = ($cols.length - index) % $cols.length;
	   ShowGroup(index);
   });

   $('.btn-right').click(function(){
	  clearInterval(rotater);
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
	  ShowGroup(index);
   });
   
   $('.ribbon h4').click(function(){
 	  window.location = '/tfc';
   });

});
</script>

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=4920',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("Now Drafting").show();
	  else
	  // if > 85% go red
	  // if > 66% go yellow
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
	  //$(".GaugeMeter").gaugeMeter({ text: json['entries'] + ' / ' + json['max_entries'] });
   });
});

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=924',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['no_meter']) return;
	  if ('true' != json['open']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Starts " + json['open']).addClass('comingsoon').show();
	  else if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Playoff Drafts").show();
	  else
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
   });
   requestAnimationFrame(animate);
});

    const rotatingDiv = document.getElementById("rotatingDiv");

    let startTime = null;
    const amplitude = 3; // Maximum rotation angle in degrees
    const frequency = 1; // Oscillations per second

    // Animation function
    function animate(timestamp) {
      if (!startTime) startTime = timestamp;
      const elapsedTime = (timestamp - startTime) / 1000; // Convert to seconds

      // Calculate the rotation angle using a sine wave
      const angle = -45 + amplitude * Math.sin(2 * Math.PI * frequency * elapsedTime);

      // Apply the rotation angle to the div using CSS transform
      $('div[game=924] .sellout').css('transform','rotate(' + angle + 'deg)');

      // Continue the animation
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
	}

</script></div><div class="game-card col-xxl-3 col-xl-4 col-md-6 col-12 mx-auto"><div class="card mx-auto">

$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=710',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['no_meter']) return;
	  if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=710] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 15)
		  $('div[game=710] .sellout').html("Play Now").show();
	  else
		  $('div[game=710] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
   });
});

<script>
	
$(document).ready(function(){
   const $cols = $('.games-row .game-card');
   let groupSize = 1;
   let index = 0;
   function ShowGroup(start) {
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;
         
      $cols.hide();
      //if (start + groupSize >= $cols.length) index = 0;
      
//$('#theindex').html(index + '/' + $cols.length);

      for (let i = 0; i < groupSize; i++) {
         const current = (start + i) % $cols.length;
         $cols.eq(current).fadeIn(500);
      }
   }
   
   ShowGroup(index);
   
   var rotater = setInterval(() => {
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
     ShowGroup(index);
   }, 5000);
   
   $(window).on( "resize", function() { 
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;   
      ShowGroup(index); 
   });   

   $('.btn-left').click(function(){
 	   clearInterval(rotater);
      index = (index - groupSize) % $cols.length;
      if (index < 0) index = ($cols.length - index) % $cols.length;
	   ShowGroup(index);
   });

   $('.btn-right').click(function(){
	  clearInterval(rotater);
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
	  ShowGroup(index);
   });
   
   $('.ribbon h4').click(function(){
 	  window.location = '/tfc';
   });

});
</script>

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=4920',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html("Now Drafting").show();
	  else
	  // if > 85% go red
	  // if > 66% go yellow
		  $('div[game=4920] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
	  //$(".GaugeMeter").gaugeMeter({ text: json['entries'] + ' / ' + json['max_entries'] });
   });
});

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
   $.getJSON('/site/sellout-meter.php?GAMEID=924',function(json) {
	  if ('true' == json['no_meter']) return;
	  if ('true' != json['open']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Starts " + json['open']).addClass('comingsoon').show();
	  else if ('true' == json['closed']) 
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("CLOSED").addClass('closed').show();
	  else if (json['sold_percentage'] < 25)
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html("Playoff Drafts").show();
	  else
		  $('div[game=924] .sellout').html(json['sold_percentage'] + "% Soldout").show();
   });
   requestAnimationFrame(animate);
});

    const rotatingDiv = document.getElementById("rotatingDiv");

    let startTime = null;
    const amplitude = 3; // Maximum rotation angle in degrees
    const frequency = 1; // Oscillations per second

    // Animation function
    function animate(timestamp) {
      if (!startTime) startTime = timestamp;
      const elapsedTime = (timestamp - startTime) / 1000; // Convert to seconds

      // Calculate the rotation angle using a sine wave
      const angle = -45 + amplitude * Math.sin(2 * Math.PI * frequency * elapsedTime);

      // Apply the rotation angle to the div using CSS transform
      $('div[game=924] .sellout').css('transform','rotate(' + angle + 'deg)');

      // Continue the animation
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
	}

</script></div><div class="game-card col-xxl-3 col-xl-4 col-md-6 col-12 mx-auto"><div class="card mx-auto">

<script>
	
$(document).ready(function(){
   const $cols = $('.games-row .game-card');
   let groupSize = 1;
   let index = 0;
   function ShowGroup(start) {
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;
         
      $cols.hide();
      //if (start + groupSize >= $cols.length) index = 0;
      
//$('#theindex').html(index + '/' + $cols.length);

      for (let i = 0; i < groupSize; i++) {
         const current = (start + i) % $cols.length;
         $cols.eq(current).fadeIn(500);
      }
   }
   
   ShowGroup(index);
   
   var rotater = setInterval(() => {
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
     ShowGroup(index);
   }, 5000);
   
   $(window).on( "resize", function() { 
      if ($('#show-4').is(':visible')) groupSize = 4;
      if ($('#show-3').is(':visible')) groupSize = 3;
      if ($('#show-2').is(':visible')) groupSize = 2;   
      ShowGroup(index); 
   });   

   $('.btn-left').click(function(){
 	   clearInterval(rotater);
      index = (index - groupSize) % $cols.length;
      if (index < 0) index = ($cols.length - index) % $cols.length;
	   ShowGroup(index);
   });

   $('.btn-right').click(function(){
	  clearInterval(rotater);
     index = (index + groupSize) % $cols.length;
	  ShowGroup(index);
   });
   
   $('.ribbon h4').click(function(){
 	  window.location = '/tfc';
   });

});
</script>
